# Data Flow Q&A: Envoy Request Routing

**Repository:** envoyproxy/envoy
**Task Type:** Data Flow Q&A (investigation only — no code changes)

## Background

Envoy is a high-performance proxy that routes HTTP requests from downstream clients to upstream services. Understanding the complete path from the initial TCP accept through filter processing to the final upstream connection is critical for working with Envoy's architecture.

## Task

Trace the complete path of a single HTTP request from the moment a downstream client TCP connection is accepted through filter chain processing, route resolution, upstream cluster selection, and connection establishment. Identify every key transformation point, component boundary crossing, and state change.

## Questions

Answer ALL of the following questions about Envoy's request routing flow:

### Q1: Listener Accept to Network Filter Chain

When a downstream client establishes a TCP connection to Envoy, how does the request travel from socket accept to network filter processing?

- Which component accepts the incoming TCP connection?
- How does Envoy select which network filter chain to apply based on connection properties?
- At what point does the connection get handed to the HTTP Connection Manager (HCM)?
- What triggers the initial `onData()` call when bytes arrive?

### Q2: HTTP Parsing and Filter Chain Iteration

Once bytes arrive at the HCM, how does Envoy parse HTTP and iterate through filters?

- How does the codec parse the byte stream into HTTP headers/body?
- When is the `ActiveStream` created and how does it relate to filter iteration?
- How does the `FilterManager` determine the order of decoder filter execution?
- What filter return values can stop or continue iteration?

### Q3: Route Resolution and Upstream Selection

When the router filter is invoked, how does it select the upstream destination?

- How does the router determine which route configuration to use?
- What is the sequence of operations that resolves a route entry to a specific upstream cluster?
- How does the router select a specific upstream host from the cluster?
- What triggers the creation of the upstream connection?

### Q4: Upstream Connection and Data Flow

Once an upstream host is selected, how does Envoy establish the connection and forward the request?

- How does the connection pool provide or create an upstream connection?
- What component actually writes the HTTP request to the upstream socket?
- How does the response flow back from upstream through the filter chain?
- At what points does the encoder filter chain get invoked vs. the decoder filter chain?

## Output Requirements

Write your answer to `/logs/agent/investigation.md` with the following structure:

```
# Envoy Request Routing Flow

## Q1: Listener Accept to Network Filter Chain
<answer with specific file paths, class names, and method references>

## Q2: HTTP Parsing and Filter Chain Iteration
<answer with specific file paths, class names, and method references>

## Q3: Route Resolution and Upstream Selection
<answer with specific file paths, class names, and method references>

## Q4: Upstream Connection and Data Flow
<answer with specific file paths, class names, and method references>

## Evidence
<consolidated list of supporting file paths and line references>
```

## Constraints

- Do NOT modify any source files
- Cite specific files, classes, and methods — avoid vague or speculative answers
- Focus on the core request path, not error handling or edge cases
- Trace a single successful HTTP/1.1 request without TLS termination

Layer 5 \u2014 HTTP Codec and Stream Creation\n\n**File:** `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc`\n\n### Codec Dispatch\n\n`codec_->dispatch(data)` parses the incoming byte stream. The codec calls `decodeHeaders()` on it next.\n\n### `ActiveStream::decodeHeaders()` \u2014 L1193\n\nThis is the central request processing entry point. Key steps in order:\n\n```\n1.  Record last downstream header byte received timestamp (L1200)\n2.  Validate headers (L1227): method, host, path, scheme, content-length consistency\n3.  Snap route config (L1232\u20131244):\n      - RDS: snapped_route_config_ = routeConfigProvider()->configCast()\n      - SRDS: snapScopedRouteConfig() \u2192 snapped_route_config_ per scope key\n4. Layer 6 \u2014 HTTP Filter Manager: Decode Path\n\n**File:** `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n\n### `FilterManager::decodeHeaders()` \u2014 L537\n\n```cpp\nvoid FilterManager::decodeHeaders(ActiveStreamDecoderFilter* filter,\n                                  RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream) {\n  StreamDecoderFilters::Iterator entry =\n      commonDecodePrefix(filter, FilterIterationStartState::AlwaysStartFromNext);\n\n  for (; entry != decoder_filters_.end(); entry++) {\n    state_.filter_call_state_ |= FilterCallState::DecodeHeaders;\n    (*entry)->end_stream_ = (end_stream && continue_data_entry == decoder_filters_.end());\n\n    FilterHeadersStatus status = (*entry)->decodeHeaders(headers, (*entry)->end_stream_);\n\n    state_.filter_call_state_ &= ~FilterCallState::DecodeHeaders;\n\n    const auto continue_iteration =\n        (*entry)->commonHandleAfterHeadersCallback(status, end_stream);\n\n    if (!continue_iteration && std::next(entry) != decoder_filters_.end()) {\n      maybeContinueDecoding(continue_data_entry);\n      return;  // filter stopped iteration; resume later via continueDecoding()\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Filter status semantics:**\n\n| `FilterHeadersStatus` | Behavior |\n|----------------------|----------|\n| `Continue` | Advance to next filter immediately |\n| `StopIteration` | Pause; filter must call `continueDecoding()` later |\n| `StopAllIterationAndBuffer` | Pause all; buffer body; resume on `continueDecoding()` |\n| `StopAllIterationAndWatermark` | Pause all; apply watermark; resume on `continueDecoding()` |\n| `ContinueAndDontEndStream` | Continue but suppress `end_stream` flag (filter injected body) |\n\nDecoder filters are stored in `decoder_filters_` in **forward order** (A\u2192B\u2192C). Encoder filters in `encoder_filters_` are iterated in **reverse order** (C\u2192B\u2192A) during response encoding.\n\nThe terminal decoder filter is always the **Router filter** (`Router::Filter`), which is the last entry in `decoder_filters_`.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Layer 7 \u2014 Route Resolution\n\n**File:** `source/common/router/config_impl.cc`\n\nRoute resolution is triggered by `snapped_route_config_->route(cb, headers, stream_info, stream_id)`.\n\n### `ConfigImpl::route()` \u2014 L2450 \u2192 `RouteMatcher::route()` \u2014 L2299\n\n```cpp\nRouteConstSharedPtr RouteMatcher::route(const RouteCallback& cb,\n                                        const Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers,\n                                        const StreamInfo::StreamInfo& stream_info,\n                                        uint64_t random_value) const {\n  const VirtualHostImpl* virtual_host = findVirtualHost(headers);\n  if (virtual_host) {\n    return virtual_host->getRouteFromEntries(cb, headers, stream_info, random_value);\n  }\n  return nullptr;\n}\n```\n\n### `RouteMatcher::findVirtualHost()` \u2014 L2251\n\nVirtual host lookup against the `Host` / `:authority` header:\n\n```\n1. Fast path: if only default_virtual_host_ exists, return it immediately\n2. Exact match: virtual_hosts_.find(host)  (hash map, O(1))\n3. Wildcard suffix: findWildcardVirtualHost() with suffix substring\n   - \"foo-bar.baz.com\" matches \"*-bar.baz.com\" before \"*.baz.com\"\n   - Ordered by wildcard length descending (longest match wins)\n4. Wildcard prefix: findWildcardVirtualHost() with prefix substring\n5. Default virtual host (catch-all \"*\")\n```\n\n### `VirtualHostImpl::getRouteFromEntries()` \u2014 L2116\n\n```cpp\nRouteConstSharedPtr VirtualHostImpl::getRouteFromEntries(...) const {\n  // SSL redirect check\n  if (ssl_requirements_ == SslRequirements::All && scheme != \"https\") {\n    return ssl_redirect_route_;\n  }\n\n  if (matcher_) {\n    // Unified matcher path: evaluate MatchTree<HttpMatchingData>\n    Http::Matching::HttpMatchingDataImpl data(stream_info);\n    data.onRequestHeaders(headers);\n    auto match = Matcher::evaluateMatch<Http::HttpMatchingData>(*matcher_, data);\n    if (match.result_) {\n      return getRouteFromRoutes(cb, headers, stream_info, random_value, {route_action.route()});\n    }\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n\n  // Linear scan of routes_ list\n  return getRouteFromRoutes(cb, headers, stream_info, random_value, routes_);\n}\n```\n\n### `RouteEntryImplBase::matchRoute()` \u2014 L913\n\nEach route entry's `matches()` method calls `matchRoute()` which checks all configured predicates:\n\n```cpp\nbool RouteEntryImplBase::matchRoute(const Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers,\n                                    const StreamInfo::StreamInfo& stream_info,\n                                    uint64_t random_value) const {\n  bool matches = true;\n  matches &= evaluateRuntimeMatch(random_value);   // runtime fraction\n  matches &= Grpc::Common::isGrpcRequestHeaders(headers);  // if grpc_only\n  matches &= Http::HeaderUtility::matchHeaders(headers, config_headers_);  // header matchers\n  matches &= ConfigUtility::matchQueryParams(query_parameters, config_query_parameters_);\n  matches &= evaluateTlsContextMatch(stream_info);  // TLS metadata\n  matches &= m.match(stream_info.dynamicMetadata());  // dynamic metadata\n  matches &= m->match(stream_info.filterState());     // filter state\n  return matches;\n}\n```\n\n**Path matching subtypes** (selected at config load time, L71\u2013L96):\n\n| Config field | Implementation class |\n|---|---|\n| `prefix` | `PrefixRouteEntryImpl` |\n| `path` | `PathRouteEntryImpl` |\n| `safe_regex` | `RegexRouteEntryImpl` |\n| `connect_matcher` | `ConnectRouteEntryImpl` |\n| `path_separated_prefix` | `PathSeparatedPrefixRouteEntryImpl` |\n| `path_match_policy` (URI template) | `UriTemplateMatcherRouteEntryImpl` |\n\n---\n\n## 9. Layer 8 \u2014 Router Filter: Cluster Selection and Connection Pool\n\n**File:** `source/common/router/router.cc`\n\n### `Router::Filter::decodeHeaders()` \u2014 L445\n\nThis is the terminal decoder filter. It performs the full upstream dispatch sequence:\n\n#### Step 1: Route retrieval (L468)\n```cpp\nroute_ = callbacks_->route();\nif (!route_) {\n  callbacks_->sendLocalReply(Http::Code::NotFound, \"\", ...);\n  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration;\n}\n```\n\n`callbacks_->route()` returns the cached route set by `refreshCachedRoute()` in HCM.\n\n#### Step 2: Direct response check (L480)\n```cpp\nconst auto* direct_response = route_->directResponseEntry();\nif (direct_response != nullptr) {\n  // Send configured response body/code without upstream\n  callbacks_->sendLocalReply(direct_response->responseCode(), ...);\n  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration;\n}\n```\n\n#### Step 3: Cluster lookup (L518)\n```cpp\nroute_entry_ = route_->routeEntry();\nUpstream::ThreadLocalCluster* cluster =\n    config_->cm_.getThreadLocalCluster(route_entry_->clusterName());\nif (!cluster) {\n  callbacks_->sendLocalReply(route_entry_->clusterNotFoundResponseCode(), ...);\n  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration;\n}\ncluster_ = cluster->info();\n```\n\n`getThreadLocalCluster()` performs a hash map lookup in the thread-local cluster snapshot. This is O(1) and lock-free \u2014 the snapshot is updated atomically when xDS pushes cluster changes.\n\n#### Step 4: Pre-flight checks (L567\u2013L638)\n- Maintenance mode check \u2192 503\n- DROP_OVERLOAD check \u2192 503\n- Auto-SNI/SAN population from Host header into filter state\n- Transport socket options from downstream filter state\n\n#### Step 5: Host selection (L664)\n```cpp\nauto host_selection_response = cluster->chooseHost(this);\n```\n\n`cluster->chooseHost(this)` delegates to `ClusterEntry::chooseHost()` (cluster_manager_impl.cc L2205):\n\n```cpp\nHostSelectionResponse ClusterEntry::chooseHost(LoadBalancerContext* context) {\n  // 1. The LB operates on the thread-local priority set snapshot.\n\n**Async host selection (L665\u2013L703):** If the LB returns a `cancelable` handle (e.g., for ODCDS \u2014 on-demand cluster discovery), the router returns `StopAllIterationAndWatermark` and registers `on_host_selected_` callback. When host selection completes, `onAsyncHostSelection()` fires and calls `continueDecoding()`.\n\n#### Step 6: `continueDecodeHeaders()` \u2014 L714\n\n```cpp\nHttp::FilterHeadersStatus `ClusterEntry::httpConnPoolImpl()` \u2014 cluster_manager_impl.cc L2103\n\n```cpp\nConnPoolsContainer::ConnPools::PoolOptRef pool =\n    container.pools_->getPool(priority, hash_key, [&]() {\n parameters or socket options are never pooled together.\n\n---\n\n## 10. Layer 9 \u2014 Connection Pool\n\n**File:** `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc`\n\n### `UpstreamRequest::acceptHeadersFromRouter()` \u2014 upstream_request.cc L380\n\n```cpp\nvoid UpstreamRequest::acceptHeadersFromRouter(bool end_stream) {\n  router_sent_end_stream_ = end_stream;\n\n  // Pause body forwarding for CONNECT until upstream sends 200\n  if (headers->getMethodValue() == Http::Headers::get().MethodValues.Connect) {\n    paused_for_connect_ = true;\n  }\n\n  // Kick off connection pool acquisition\n  conn_pool_->newStream(this);\n}\n```\n\n### `ConnPoolImplBase::newStreamImpl()` \u2014 L294\n\n```cpp\nConnectionPool::Cancellable* ConnPoolImplBase::newStreamImpl(AttachContext& context,\n                                                             bool can_send_early_data) {\n  // Fast path: ready (fully connected) client available\n  if (!ready_clients_.empty()) {\n    ActiveClient& client = *ready_clients_.front();\n    attachStreamToClient(client, context);\n    tryCreateNewConnections();  // preconnect for next request\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n\n  // HTTP/3 0-RTT early data path\n  if (can_send_early_data && !early_data_clients_.empty()) {\n    ActiveClient& client = *early_data_clients_.front();\n    attachStreamToClient(client, context);\n    tryCreateNewConnections();\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n\n  // Pending request circuit breaker\n  if (!host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).pendingRequests().canCreate()) {\n    onPoolFailure(nullptr, \"\", ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::Overflow, context);\n    host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_pending_overflow_.inc();\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n\n  // Queue the stream and try to create a new connection\n  ConnectionPool::Cancellable* pending = newPendingStream(context, can_send_early_data);\n  const ConnectionResult result = tryCreateNewConnections();\n  // ...\n  return pending;\n}\n```\n\n### `ConnPoolImplBase::tryCreateNewConnection()` \u2014 L164\n\n```cpp\nConnPoolImplBase::ConnectionResult\nConnPoolImplBase::tryCreateNewConnection(float global_preconnect_ratio) {\n  if (!shouldCreateNewConnection(global_preconnect_ratio)) {\n    return ConnectionResult::ShouldNotConnect;\n  }\n\n  const bool can_create_connection = host_->canCreateConnection(priority_);\n  // canCreateConnection() checks the upstream_cx circuit breaker\n\n  if (can_create_connection || (ready_clients_.empty() && busy_clients_.empty() &&\n                                connecting_clients_.empty() && early_data_clients_.empty())) {\n    ActiveClientPtr client = instantiateActiveClient();\n    // instantiateActiveClient() calls host->createConnection()\n    incrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(client->currentUnusedCapacity(), *client);\n    LinkedList::moveIntoList(std::move(client), owningList(client->state()));\n    return can_create_connection ? ConnectionResult::CreatedNewConnection\n                                 : ConnectionResult::CreatedButRateLimited;\n  }\n  return ConnectionResult::NoConnectionRateLimited;\n}\n```\n\n**Circuit breaker bypass:** Even when `upstream_cx` circuit breaker is tripped, if there are zero connections to this host (all lists empty), one connection is always created. This prevents a host from becoming permanently unreachable due to circuit breaker state.\n\n### `ConnPoolImplBase::attachStreamToClient()` \u2014 L203\n\n```cpp\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::attachStreamToClient(Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient& client,\n                                            AttachContext& context) {\n  // Per-request circuit breaker check\n  if (enforceMaxRequests() &&\n      !host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).requests().canCreate()) {\n    onPoolFailure(client.real_host_description_, \"\",\n                  ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::Overflow, context);\n    return;\n  }\n\n  client.remaining_streams_--;\n  if (client.remaining_streams_ == 0) {\n    transitionActiveClientState(client, ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n  } else if (capacity == 1) {\n    transitionActiveClientState(client, ActiveClient::State::Busy);\n  }\n\n  state_.incrActiveStreams(1);\n  num_active_streams_++;\n  host_->stats().rq_total_.inc();\n  host_->stats().rq_active_.inc();\n  host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).requests().inc();\n\n  onPoolReady(client, context);  // calls UpstreamRequest::onPoolReady()\n}\n```\n\n**Client state machine:**\n\n```\nConnecting \u2500\u2500(handshake complete)\u2500\u2500\u25ba Ready\nReady \u2500\u2500(stream attached, capacity > 1)\u2500\u2500\u25ba Ready\nReady \u2500\u2500(stream attached, capacity == 1)\u2500\u2500\u25ba Busy\nBusy \u2500\u2500(stream closed, capacity > 0)\u2500\u2500\u25ba Ready\nReady/Busy \u2500\u2500(remaining_streams == 0)\u2500\u2500\u25ba Draining\nDraining \u2500\u2500(all streams closed)\u2500\u2500\u25ba close()\n```\n\n---\n\n## 11. Layer 10 \u2014 Upstream Connection Establishment\n\n**Files:**  \n- `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc`  \n- `source/common/network/connection_impl.cc`\n\n### `HostImplBase::createConnection()` \u2014 upstream_impl.cc L582\n\nCalled by `instantiateActiveClient()` in the connection pool:\n\n```cpp\nHost::CreateConnectionData HostImplBase::createConnection(\n    Event::Dispatcher& dispatcher, const ClusterInfo& cluster,\n    const Network::Address::InstanceConstSharedPtr& address,\n    const SharedConstAddressVector& address_list_or_null,\n    Network::UpstreamTransportSocketFactory& socket_factory,\n    const Network::ConnectionSocket::OptionsSharedPtr& options,\n    Network::TransportSocketOptionsConstSharedPtr transport_socket_options,\n    HostDescriptionConstSharedPtr host) {\n\n  auto source_address_selector = cluster.getUpstreamLocalAddressSelector();\n\n  Network::ClientConnectionPtr connection;\n\n  if (proxy_address.has_value()) {\n    // HTTP/1.1 CONNECT proxy: upstream_local_address.address_,\n        socket_factory.createTransportSocket(transport_socket_options, host),\n        upstream_local_address.socket_options_,\n        transport_socket_options);\n  }\n\n  connection->setBufferLimits(cluster.perConnectionBufferLimitBytes());\n  cluster.createNetworkFilterChain(*connection);  // upstream network filters\n  return {std::move(connection), `HappyEyeballsConnectionImpl` attempts IPv6 first, then IPv4 after a delay (default 300ms), uses whichever connects first.\n3. **Standard:** `ClientConnectionImpl` with a single resolved address.\n\n### `ClientConnectionImpl::connect()` \u2014 connection_impl.cc L1090\n\n```cpp\nvoid ClientConnectionImpl::connect() {\n  const Api::SysCallIntResult result = connect (loopback, Unix socket)\n    ASSERT(connecting_);\n    return;\n  }\n\n  if (result.errno_ == SOCKET_ERROR_IN_PROGRESS) {\n    // Normal async connect: EINPROGRESS\n    ASSERT(connecting_);\n    // libevent will fire Write event when connect() completes\n  } else {\n    // Immediate error\n    immediate_error_event_ = ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose;\n    ioHandle().activateFileEvents(Event::FileReadyType::Write);\n  }\n}\n```\n\nFor TLS, `transport_socket_->connect()` calls the underlying `RawBufferSocket::connect()` which issues the kernel The TLS handshake begins after the TCP connection is established (on the Write event).\n\n### `ClientConnectionImpl::onConnected()` \u2014 L1143\n\n```cpp\nvoid ClientConnectionImpl::onConnected() {\n  stream_info_.upstreamInfo()->upstreamTiming().onUpstreamConnectComplete(\n      dispatcher_.timeSource());\n  socket_->connectionInfoProvider().maybeSetInterfaceName(ioHandle());\n  ConnectionImpl::onConnected();  // fires transport_socket_->onConnected()\n}\n```\n\n`ConnectionImpl::onConnected()` (L348) calls `transport_socket_->onConnected()`. Layer 11 \u2014 Response Path\n\n**Files:**  \n- `source/common/router/upstream_request.cc`  \n- `source/common/router/router.cc`  \n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n\n### Upstream Response Reception\n\nThe upstream codec parses the response and calls back into `UpstreamRequest` via the `UpstreamToDownstream` interface:\n\n```cpp\n// upstream_request.cc L306\nvoid UpstreamToDownstreamImpl::decodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMapPtr&& headers, bool end_stream) {\n  parent_.onUpstreamHeaders(response_code, std::move(headers), *this, end_stream);\n}\n\n// upstream_request.cc L326\nvoid UpstreamToDownstreamImpl::decodeData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) {\n  parent_.onUpstreamData(data, *this, end_stream);\n}\n\n// upstream_request.cc L339\nvoid UpstreamToDownstreamImpl::decodeTrailers(ResponseTrailerMapPtr&& trailers) {\n  parent_.onUpstreamTrailers(std::move(trailers), *this);\n}\n```\n\n### `Router::Filter::onUpstreamHeaders()` \u2014 router.cc L1652\n\n```cpp\nvoid Filter::onUpstreamHeaders(uint64_t response_code,\n                               Http::ResponseHeaderMapPtr&& headers,\n                               UpstreamRequest& upstream_request, bool end_stream) {\n  modify_headers_(*headers); entry != encoder_filters_.end(); entry++) {\n    FilterHeadersStatus status = (*entry)->handle_->encodeHeaders(headers, (*entry)->end_stream_);\n    const auto continue_iteration =\n        (*entry)->commonHandleAfterHeadersCallback(status, end_stream);\n    if (!continue_iteration) {\n      maybeContinueEncoding(continue_data_entry);\n      return;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Validate required response headers (e.g., :status)\n  const auto status = HeaderUtility::checkRequiredResponseHeaders(headers);\n  if (!status.ok()) {\n    sendLocalReply(Http::Code::BadGateway, status.message(), ...);\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Write to downstream codec\n  filter_manager_callbacks_.encodeHeaders(headers, modified_end_stream);\n  maybeEndEncode(modified_end_stream);\n}\n```\n\nEncoder filters iterate in **reverse order** (C\u2192B\u2192A). After all encoder filters pass, `filter_manager_callbacks_.encodeHeaders()` writes the response headers to the downstream HTTP codec, which serializes them to the downstream TCP connection.\n\n---\n\n## 13. Complete Call Chain Summary\n\nThe following is the complete ordered call chain for a single HTTP/1.1 request:\n\n```\n[DOWNSTREAM \u2014 REQUEST PATH]\n\n 1. libevent fires Read event on listener socket fd\n    \u2514\u2500 TcpListenerImpl::onSocketEvent()                    tcp_listener_impl.cc:56\n         \u251c\u2500 socket_->ioHandle().accept()                   [kernel accept() syscall]\n         \u251c\u2500 rejectCxOverGlobalLimit()                      tcp_listener_impl.cc:21\n         \u2514\u2500 cb_.onAccept()                                 [AcceptedSocketImpl created]\n\n 2. ActiveTcpListener::onAccept()                          active_tcp_listener.cc:80\n    \u2514\u2500 listenerConnectionLimitReached() check\n    \u2514\u2500 onAcceptWorker()                                    active_tcp_listener.cc:108\n         \u251c\u2500 connection_balancer_.pickTargetHandler()       [may post to another worker]\n         \u2514\u2500 ActiveTcpSocket created\n         \u2514\u2500 onSocketAccepted()                             active_stream_listener_base.h:85\n\n 3. filterChainFactory().createListenerFilterChain()       [TLS Inspector, HTTP Inspector, etc.]\n    \u2514\u2500 ActiveTcpSocket::startFilterChain()                 active_tcp_socket.h:74\n    \u2514\u2500 ActiveTcpSocket::continueFilterChain()              active_tcp_socket.cc:111\n         \u251c\u2500 (*iter_)->onAccept(*this)                      [each listener filter]\n         \u2502    \u2514\u2500 StopIteration \u2192 createListenerFilterBuffer() \u2192 peek bytes \u2192 resume\n         \u2514\u2500 [all filters pass] \u2192 newConnection()           active_tcp_socket.cc:185\n\n 4. ActiveTcpSocket::newConnection()                       active_tcp_socket.cc:185\n    \u251c\u2500 [optional] redirect to another listener (TPROXY)\n    \u2514\u2500 listener_.newConnection()                           active_stream_listener_base.cc:38\n\n 5. ActiveStreamListenerBase::newConnection()              active_stream_listener_base.cc:38\n    \u251c\u2500 filterChainManager().findFilterChain()              filter_chain_manager_impl.cc:514\n    \u2502    \u2514\u2500 Multi-level match: port\u2192IP\u2192SNI\u2192transport\u2192ALPN\u2192srcIP\u2192srcPort\n    \u251c\u2500 filter_chain->transportSocketFactory()\n    \u2502    .createDownstreamTransportSocket()                [SslSocket or RawBufferSocket]\n    \u251c\u2500 dispatcher().createServerConnection()               [ServerConnectionImpl]\n    \u2514\u2500 filterChainFactory().createNetworkFilterChain()     [instantiates HCM]\n\n 6.
